2. The lock requires a 4-digit code.
3. Considering the tear sides as indicators of position placement:
   - Paper1 ('52') torn left suggests placing its digits in the latter half.
   - Paper2 ('14') torn right suggests placing its digits in the former half.
4. Combining them, '14' (from paper2) comes first, followed by '52' (from paper1), forming 1452.
5. Testing this combination unlocks door2.

The code for door2 is **1452**.

Step-by-step explanation:

1. Upon entering room2, two papers are found with numbers: '52' (torn left) and '14' (torn right).
2. The lock requires a 4-digit code.
3. Considering the tear sides as indicators of position placement:
   - Paper1 ('52') torn left suggests placing its digits in the latter half.
   - Paper2 ('14') torn right suggests placing its digits in the former half.
4. Combining them, '14' (from paper2) comes first, followed by '52' (from paper1), forming 1452.
5. Testing this combination unlocks door2.
